## Idea

Given a [cospan of types](foundation.cospans.md)

```text
  f : A → X ← B : g,
```

we can form the
{{#concept "standard pullback" Disambiguation="types" Agda=standard-pullback}}
`A ×_X B` satisfying
[the universal property of the pullback](foundation-core.universal-property-pullbacks.md)
of the cospan, completing the diagram

```text
  A ×_X B ------> B
     | ⌟          |
     |            | g
     |            |
     v            v
     A ---------> X.
           f
```

The standard pullback consists of [pairs](foundation.dependent-pair-types.md)
`a : A` and `b : B` such that `f a ＝ g b` agree

```text
  A ×_X B := Σ (a : A) (b : B), (f a ＝ g b),
```

thus the standard [cone](foundation.cones-over-cospans.md) consists of the
canonical projections.

## Properties

### Being a pullback is a property

### Pullbacks are closed under exponentiation

Given a pullback square

```text
          f'
    C ---------> B
    | ⌟          |
  g'|            | g
    |            |
    v            v
    A ---------> X
          f
```

then the exponentiated square given by postcomposition

```text
                f' ∘ -
      (S → C) ---------> (S → B)
         |                  |
  g' ∘ - |                  | g ∘ -
         |                  |
         v                  v
      (S → A) ---------> (S → X)
                f ∘ -
```

is a pullback square for any type `S`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="postcomp-cone"></a><a id="3571" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#3571" class="Function">postcomp-cone</a> <a id="3585" class="Symbol">:</a>

</pre>
### Identity types can be presented as pullbacks

Identity types fit into pullback squares

```text
 (x ＝ y) ----> 1
    | ⌟         |
    |           | y
    v           v
    1 --------> A.
          x
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6697" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6704" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6704" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="6708" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6709" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6709" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6711" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6713" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6718" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6720" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6721" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6721" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6723" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6725" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6728" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6709" class="Bound">l</a><a id="6729" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6731" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6732" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6732" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6734" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6734" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6736" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6738" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#6721" class="Bound">A</a><a id="6739" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="6743" class="Keyword">where</a>

        <a id="11463" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="11465" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#9021" class="Function">is-equiv-map-equiv-standard-pullback-htpy</a> <a id="11507" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#9875" class="Bound">Hf</a> <a id="11510" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#9904" class="Bound">Hg</a><a id="11512" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
In the following part we will relate the type `htpy-parallel-cone` to the
identity type of cones. Here we will rely on
[function extensionality](foundation-core.function-extensionality.md).

<pre class="Agda"><a id="11718" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="11725" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#11725" class="Module">_</a>

### Dependent products of pullbacks are pullbacks

Given a family of pullback squares, their dependent product is again a pullback
square.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="21539" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="21546" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21546" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="21550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21551" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21551" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="21554" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21554" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="21557" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21557" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="21560" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21560" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="21563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21565" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="21570" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21572" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21573" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21573" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="21575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21577" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="21580" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21551" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="21582" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="21586" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21587" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21587" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21591" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21573" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="21593" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21595" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="21598" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21554" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="21600" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21602" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21603" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21603" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="21605" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21607" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21573" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="21609" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21611" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="21614" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21557" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="21616" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21618" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21619" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21619" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="21621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21623" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21573" class="Bound">I</a> <a id="21625" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21627" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="21630" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#21560" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="21632" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Coproducts of pullbacks are pullbacks

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24696" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24703" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24703" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="24707" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24708" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24708" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="24711" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24711" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="24714" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24714" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="24717" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24717" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a> <a id="24721" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24721" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a> <a id="24725" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#24725" class="Bound">l3&#39;</a> <a id="24729" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24731" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="24736" class="Symbol">}</a>

### In a commuting cube where the vertical maps are equivalences, the bottom square is a pullback if and only if the top square is a pullback

<pre class="Agda"><a id="31760" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="31767" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#31767" class="Module">_</a>

            <a id="35097" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#34006" class="Bound">is-equiv-hC</a> <a id="35109" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#33982" class="Bound">is-equiv-hA</a><a id="35120" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### In a commuting cube where the maps from back-right to front-left are equivalences, the back-right square is a pullback if and only if the front-left square is a pullback

<pre class="Agda"><a id="35312" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="35319" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35319" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="35323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35324" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35324" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="35327" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35327" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="35330" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35330" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="35333" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35333" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="35336" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35336" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a> <a id="35340" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35340" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a> <a id="35344" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35344" class="Bound">l3&#39;</a> <a id="35348" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35348" class="Bound">l4&#39;</a> <a id="35352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35354" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="35359" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="35363" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35364" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35364" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35366" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35368" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="35371" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35324" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="35373" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35375" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35376" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35376" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35380" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="35383" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35327" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="35385" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35387" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35388" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35388" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="35390" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35392" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="35395" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35330" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="35397" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35399" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35400" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35400" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="35402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35404" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="35407" href="foundation.pullbacks.html#35333" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="35409" class="Symbol">}</a>
